                          <span className={`pill ${paymentStatusClass(item.status)}`}>{paymentStatusLabel(item.status)}</span>,
                          item.paid_at ? formatDateTime(item.paid_at) : "-",
                          formatDateTime(item.created_at),
                          <button
                            className="secondary-button small-button"
                            disabled={busyAction === `order-${item.order_no}`}
                            onClick={() => handleLoadOrderDetail(item.order_no)}
                            type="button"
                          >
                            йҸҢгғ§ж№…з’ҒгҲ еҙҹ
                          </button>,
                        ])}
                        emptyText="еЁҢв„ғж№Ғз»—п№ҖжӮҺйҸүвҖІж¬ўйҗЁеӢ¬ж•№еЁҶжҚҗо…№йҚ—жӣҳвӮ¬?
                      />
                      <PagerControls
                        page={paymentOrders?.page ?? 1}
                        total={paymentOrders?.total ?? 0}
                        pageSize={paymentOrders?.page_size ?? adminPageSize}
                        onChange={setPaymentPage}
                      />
                    </div>

                    {selectedOrderDetail ? (
                      <article className="content-card import-panel-card">
                        <div className="section-toolbar">
                          <h2>з’ҒгҲ еҙҹз’ҮпёҪе„Ҹ</h2>
                          <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={() => setSelectedOrderDetail(null)} type="button">
                            йҸҖжғ°жҚЈ
                          </button>
                        </div>
                        <div className="detail-grid">
                          <div>
                            <dt>з’ҒгҲ еҙҹйҚҷ?/dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.order_no}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/dt>
                            <dd>
                              <span className={`pill ${paymentStatusClass(selectedOrderDetail.order.status)}`}>
                                {paymentStatusLabel(selectedOrderDetail.order.status)}
                              </span>
                            </dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>зҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ</dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.customer_ref}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>жөјж°¬жҶійҸӮи§„о”Қ</dt>
                            <dd>{formatPlanLabel(selectedOrderDetail.order.plan_key)}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҺөвӮ¬зҒһзӮөоқ–йҗ©?/dt>
                            <dd>{formatSubjectLabel(selectedOrderDetail.order.subject_key)}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>й–ІжҲҰо–Ӯ</dt>
                            <dd>{formatPrice(selectedOrderDetail.order.amount_cents)}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҸҖоҲҷзІҜеЁ“зҠ»дәҫ</dt>
                            <dd>{formatPaymentProviderLabel(selectedOrderDetail.order.provider)}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>еЁ“зҠ»дәҫеЁҙдҪ№жҢүйҚҷ?/dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.provider_trade_no || "-"}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҚ’ж¶ҳзј“йҸғе •жЈҝ</dt>
                            <dd>{formatDateTime(selectedOrderDetail.order.created_at)}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҸҮеӯҳжҹҠйҸғе •жЈҝ</dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.updated_at ? formatDateTime(selectedOrderDetail.order.updated_at) : "-"}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>йҸҖоҲҷзІҜйҸғе •жЈҝ</dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.paid_at ? formatDateTime(selectedOrderDetail.order.paid_at) : "-"}</dd>
                          </div>
                          <div>
                            <dt>жқ©еӣЁж№ЎйҸғе •жЈҝ</dt>
                            <dd>{selectedOrderDetail.order.expires_at ? formatDateTime(selectedOrderDetail.order.expires_at) : "-"}</dd>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        {selectedOrderDetail.order.description ? (
                          <div className="feedback-banner">ж¶“е¬Әеҙҹз’Үеӯҳж§‘й”ӣжӯҝselectedOrderDetail.order.description}</div>
                        ) : null}
                        {selectedOrderDetail.order.error_message ? (
                          <div className="feedback-banner feedback-error">йҸҖоҲҷзІҜжҫ¶иҫ«и§ҰйҚҳзҶ·жҙңй”ӣжӯҝselectedOrderDetail.order.error_message}</div>
                        ) : null}
                        {selectedOrderDetail.subscription ? (
                          <div className="feedback-banner feedback-success">
                            е®ёжҸ’еҸ§й‘ұж–ҫзҙ°йҚӣжЁ»жҪҲйҗ©е©Ҹзҙ°зҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ {selectedOrderDetail.subscription.customer_ref}й”ӣеІҖе§ёйҺ¬дә„" "}
                            {subscriptionStatusLabel(selectedOrderDetail.subscription.status)}
                            {selectedOrderDetail.subscription.current_period_end
                              ? `й”ӣеұҫж№ҒйҸҒе ҹж№Ўй‘·?${formatDateTime(selectedOrderDetail.subscription.current_period_end)}`
                              : "й”ӣеұҪз¶ӢйҚ“е¶„иҙҹй—ҖжҢҺж№ЎйҸҲеӨӢжҷҘ"}
                          </div>
                        ) : (
                          <div className="feedback-banner">иӨ°ж’іеў з’ҒгҲ еҙҹжқ©жЁ»з—…йҸҲеӨҠеҸ§й‘ұж–ҝеҹҢжөјж°¬жҶійҸүеҶӘжіӯз’Ғжқҝз¶ҚйҠҶ?/div>
                        )}
                      </article>
                    ) : null}
                  </div>
                ) : null}
              </div>
            </section>
          ) : null}

          {activeSection === "memberships" ? (
            <section className="admin-section">
              <div className="section-header">
                <div>
                  <p className="section-eyebrow">жөјж°¬жҶійҸҲе¶…е§ҹ</p>
                  <h1>жөјж°¬жҶійҗҳиҲөвӮ¬дҪөвӮ¬дҪ№ж№ҒйҸҒе ҹж№Ўж¶“еәқжұүе®ёгғҘоҳ©йҗһ?/h1>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="admin-card-grid">
                <article className="content-card">
                  <h2>з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈжөјж°¬жҶійҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/h2>
                  <p className="helper-text">
                    жө еәқз¬…йҸӮйҖӣзҙ°йҚӣжЁҝоҶҮиӨ°жӣһеһӘзҗӣг„§еҒЈйҚ‘зғ©вӮ¬ж»ҶзҡҹйҸҒзІ№вӮ¬жҝҶжӮ—й”ӣеұјзҙ°жө гғҘи„Ҡз»җжҘҒжҹҹеҜ®еҝҺж…ЁйҸҖи§„жҹҹеҰ—е ӣвӮ¬дҪәе§ёйҺ¬дҪёжӢ°йҸҲеӨӢжҷҘйҸҲзҮӮзҙқйҸӮйҖӣз©¶зҖөеңӯеҸҺиӨ°ж’іеў з’Ғжқҝз¶Қжҫ¶еӢӯжӮҠйҠҶ?                  </p>
                </article>

                <article className="content-card">
                  <h2>жҫ¶еӢӯжӮҠз’Үеӯҳж§‘</h2>
                  <ul className="detail-list">
                    <li>йҺёеӨӢж№Җжөјж°¬жҶіеҜӨйёҝоҶ…зјҒеӯҳе§ўйҲҘж»ғз¶ӢйҚ“е¶Ҷж№ҮйҚ”вҖіжҮҶйҸҲзҶ·зҙ‘жҝ®е¬§вӮ¬жҝҶжӢ°йҲҘж»ғз¶ӢйҚ“е¶Ҷж№ҮйҚ”вҖіжҮҶйҸҲзҶәзІЁйҸүзҶІвӮ¬жҝ„вӮ¬?/li>
                    <li>ж¶“вӮ¬еЁҶв„ғвӮ¬СӮжӢұйҸӮо…ҹжҹҹеҰ—е ҘвӮ¬ж°¬зҲ¶ж¶“е¶үжё¶з‘•дҪёпҪһйҚҗж¬ҢвӮ¬ж»ғз¶ӢйҚ“е¶Ҷж№ҮйҚ”вҖіжҮҶйҸҲзҶәзІЁйҸүзҶІвӮ¬жҝ„вӮ¬?/li>
                    <li>йҺ¶е©„е§ёйҺ¬дҪ№ж•јж¶“иЎЎвӮ¬ж»ғеҮЎжқ©еӣЁж№ЎйҲҘжҝҮжӨӮй”ӣеұҪоӣ§йҸӢж»„з—…йҸҲеӨҠпҪһйҚҗж¬‘зІЁйҸүзҶёжӨӮй—Ӯиҫҫзҙқз»ҜиҚӨзІәжөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„ЁЛүж¶“е©Ӯз¶ӢйҚ“е¶ҶжӨӮй—Ӯж·¬вӮ¬?/li>
                    <li>йҺ¶е©„е§ёйҺ¬дҪ№ж•јж¶“иЎЎвӮ¬ж»ғеҮЎйҚҷж Ёз§·йҲҘжҝҮжӨӮй”ӣеұҪоӣ§йҸӢж»„з—…йҸҲеӨҠпҪһйҚҗж¬‘зІ“е§қгҲЎжӨӮй—Ӯиҫҫзҙқз»ҜиҚӨзІәжөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„ЁЛүж¶“е©Ӯз¶ӢйҚ“е¶ҶжӨӮй—Ӯж·¬вӮ¬?/li>
                  </ul>
                </article>
              </div>

              <article className="content-card">
                <div className="section-toolbar">
                  <h2>жөјж°¬жҶіз’Ғжқҝз¶ҚйҚ’жҘ„гҖғ</h2>
                  <div className="toolbar-controls">
                    <select
                      value={subscriptionStatusFilter}
                      onChange={(event) => {
                        setSubscriptionStatusFilter(event.target.value);
                        setSubscriptionPage(1);
                      }}
                    >
                      <option value="">йҚҸг„©е„ҙйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/option>
                      <option value="active">йҗўзҶёжҷҘж¶“?/option>
                      <option value="expired">е®ёиҢ¶з№ғйҸҲ?/option>
                      <option value="pending">еҜ°е‘Ҝж•“йҸҒ?/option>
                      <option value="cancelled">е®ёжҸ’еҪҮеЁ‘?/option>
                    </select>
                    <input
                      className="toolbar-search"
                      value={subscriptionQuery}
                      onChange={(event) => {
                        setSubscriptionQuery(event.target.value);
                        setSubscriptionPage(1);
                      }}
                      placeholder="йҺјж»…еӮЁзҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝйҺҙж Ұзҙ°йҚӣжЁ»жҹҹеҰ—?
                    />
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="table-wrap">
                  <table className="data-table">
                    <thead>
                      <tr>
                        <th>зҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ</th>
                        <th>жөјж°¬жҶійҸӮи§„о”Қ</th>
                        <th>з»үжҲ жҙ°</th>
                        <th>йҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/th>
                        <th>йҚ’зүҲж№ЎйҸғе •жЈҝ</th>
                        <th>й‘·оҒ„е§©зјҒо…ЎеһӮ</th>
                        <th>еҜ®вӮ¬й–«ж°ӯжӨӮй—Ӯ?/th>
                        <th>йҺҝе¶„з¶”</th>
                      </tr>
                    </thead>
                    <tbody>
                      {(subscriptions?.items ?? []).map((item) => (
                        <tr key={item.id}>
                          <td>{item.customer_ref}</td>
                          <td>{formatPlanLabel(item.plan_key)}</td>
                          <td>{formatSubjectLabel(item.subject_key)}</td>
                          <td>
                            <span className={`pill ${subscriptionStatusClass(item.status)}`}>{subscriptionStatusLabel(item.status)}</span>
                          </td>
                          <td>{item.current_period_end ? formatDateTime(item.current_period_end) : "й—ҖжҢҺж№ЎйҸҲеӨӢжҷҘ"}</td>
                          <td>{item.auto_renew ? "йҸ„? : "йҚҡ?}</td>
                          <td>{item.started_at ? formatDateTime(item.started_at) : "-"}</td>
                          <td>
                            <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={() => startEditSubscription(item)} type="button">
                              з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈ
                            </button>
                          </td>
                        </tr>
                      ))}
                    </tbody>
                  </table>
                  {(subscriptions?.items ?? []).length === 0 ? <div className="feedback-banner">еЁҢв„ғж№Ғз»—п№ҖжӮҺйҸүвҖІж¬ўйҗЁеӢӘзҙ°йҚӣжЁҝоҶҮиӨ°жӣҳвӮ¬?/div> : null}
                </div>
                <PagerControls
                  page={subscriptions?.page ?? 1}
                  total={subscriptions?.total ?? 0}
                  pageSize={subscriptions?.page_size ?? adminPageSize}
                  onChange={setSubscriptionPage}
                />
              </article>
            </section>
          ) : null}

          {activeSection === "mcp" ? (
            <section className="admin-section">
              <div className="section-header">
                <div>
                  <p className="section-eyebrow">MCP зҖ№жҗһе„ұйҚҷ?/p>
                  <h1>MCP е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҸүеҶ®жӘәйҠҶдҪ·зҙ°йҚӣж©ҖжЈ¬еҰІж¶—з¬Ңй–ӯвӮ¬з’ҮйЈҺзІәз’Ғ?/h1>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="import-workbench">
                <AdminSectionTabs
                  ariaLabel="MCP е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҚҗе‘ҙе„ҙзҖөиү°еҹ…"
                  currentKey={currentMCPTab}
                  items={visibleMCPTabItems}
                  onChange={setActiveMCPTab}
                />

              {canViewMCPTools && currentMCPTab === "api-tools" ? (
                <article className="content-card">
                  <div className="section-toolbar">
                    <div>
                      <h2>API йҺәгғҘеҪӣе®ёгғҘеҸҝз» пј„жӮҠ</h2>
                      <p className="helper-text">жқ©ж¬“еҷ·зјҒеӯҳе§ўйҚҡеәЎеҪҙйҚңеІҖж•ӨйҺҙеі°еҪІз‘ҷдҪәж®‘йҚ”г„ҰвӮ¬?API е®ёгғҘеҸҝй”ӣеұҫжҹҠжҫ§зӮІжӢ°зјӮж ¬з·«й–®д»ӢвӮ¬ж°із№ғеҜ®еңӯзҚҘжҫ¶еӢӯжӮҠй”ӣеұјз№ҡзҖӣжЁәжӮ—жөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„ҘжӮ“е§қгғЁз№ҳ MCP е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҚ’жҘ„гҖғйҠҶ?/p>

                      {canManageMCPTools ? (
                        <button className="primary-button" onClick={openCreateAPIConfigModal} type="button">

                        </button>
                      ) : null}
                      <input
                        className="toolbar-search"
                        value={apiConfigQuery}

                          setAPIConfigQuery(event.target.value);
                          setAPIConfigPage(1);
                        }}
                        placeholder="йҺјж»…еӮЁйҚҡе¶ҮРһйҠҶдҪёдјҗйҚҸеі°жӮ•йҺҙж §еһҺз»«?
                      />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <DataTable
                    columns={["йҚҡе¶ҮРһ", "е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҚҡ?, "йҸӮи§„зЎ¶", "йҚ’е—ҷиў«", "иӨ°жҺ‘зқҳ", "йҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?, "йҚҸо„Җзҙ‘", "йҺҝе¶„з¶”"]}
                    tableClassName="data-table api-config-table"
                    wrapClassName="table-wrap api-config-table-wrap"
                    rows={(apiConfigs?.items ?? []).map((item) => [
                      item.name,
                      item.resolved_tool_name,
                      item.method,
                      item.category || "-",
                      item.owner_name || item.owner_type || "-",
                      <span className={item.is_active ? "pill pill-success" : "pill pill-muted"}>
                        {item.is_active ? "йҚҡоҲңж•Өж¶“? : "е®ёжҸ’д» йҗў?}

                          className="secondary-button small-button"

                          }}
                          type="button"

                        <button
                          className="secondary-button small-button"
                          disabled={busyAction === `admin-api-config-delete-${item.id}`}

                          }}
                          type="button"
                        >

                    emptyText="иӨ°ж’іеў жқ©жЁ»з—…йҸҲ?API й–°е¶Үз–ҶйҠҶ?
                  />
                  <PagerControls
                    disabled={dataLoading}

              {canViewMCPTools && currentMCPTab === "tool-access" ? (

                      <p className="helper-text">з» пј„жӮҠйҚӣжЁәеҪІжө гғҘе–…зҖ№ж°¬ж‘ўжөңж¶ҳдјҗйҚҸеі°зҙ‘йҸҖдҝұвӮ¬дҪёж‘ўжөңж¶ҳдјҗйҚҸзғҪжё¶з‘•дҪ·зҙ°йҚӣжЁ»еў й‘іеҖҹзҡҹйҗўг„ЈвӮ¬?/p>
                    </div>

                      className="toolbar-search"

                        setMcpToolQuery(event.target.value);
                        setMcpToolPage(1);

                    />
                  </div>
                  <DataTable
                    columns={canManageMCPTools ? ["е®ёгғҘеҸҝ", "йҚ’е—ҷиў«", "йҸүгғҰз°®", "з’Үеӯҳж§‘", "еҜ®вӮ¬йҚҸ?, "жөјж°¬жҶі"] : ["е®ёгғҘеҸҝ", "йҚ’е—ҷиў«", "йҸүгғҰз°®", "з’Үеӯҳж§‘", "еҜ®вӮ¬йҚҸ?, "жөјж°¬жҶі"]}

                          }}
                          type="button"

                          {busyAction === `mcp-tool-${item.tool_name}` ? "жҫ¶еӢӯжӮҠж¶“?.." : item.is_enabled ? "е®ёжҸ’жғҺйҗў? : "е®ёжҸ’д» йҗў?}

                      ) : (
                        <span className={item.is_enabled ? "pill pill-success" : "pill pill-muted"}>{item.is_enabled ? "йҚҡоҲңж•Өж¶“? : "е®ёжҸ’д» йҗў?}</span>
                      ),
                      canManageMCPTools ? (
                        <button
                          className="secondary-button small-button"
                          disabled={busyAction === `mcp-tool-${item.tool_name}`}
                          onClick={() => {
                            void handleUpdateMCPToolRequirement(item.tool_name, {
                              requires_membership: !item.requires_membership,
                            });
                          }}
                          type="button"
                        >
                          {busyAction === `mcp-tool-${item.tool_name}` ? "жҫ¶еӢӯжӮҠж¶“?.." : item.requires_membership ? "й—ҮвӮ¬з‘•дҪ·зҙ°йҚӣ? : "йҚҸо„Җзҙ‘йҚҷоҲңж•Ө"}
                        </button>

                    <p className="section-eyebrow">йҗӯгғЁзҳ‘жҗҙж’ҙжһғеҰ—пҪ…е”ҙзҖ№?/p>
                    <h2>{knowledgeBasePreviewDocument.title || knowledgeBasePreviewDocument.sourceFileName}</h2>
                    <p className="helper-text">{knowledgeBasePreviewDocument.sourceFileName}</p>
                  </div>
                  <button
                    className="secondary-button"
                    onClick={() => {
                      setKnowledgeBasePreviewDocument(null);
                      setKnowledgeBasePreviewChunks([]);
                      setKnowledgeBasePreviewLoading(false);
                    }}
                    type="button"
                  >
                    йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙ
                  </button>
                </div>
                {knowledgeBasePreviewLoading ? (
                  <div className="feedback-banner">е§қпҪ…ж№ӘйҚ”зҠәжөҮйҸӮеӣЁгҖӮйҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗ...</div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="document-preview-body">
                    {knowledgeBasePreviewChunks.map((chunk) => (
                      <article className="document-preview-chunk" key={chunk.id}>
                        <div className="document-preview-chunk-meta">
                          <strong>{chunk.title || knowledgeBasePreviewDocument.title}</strong>
                          <span>йҗ—еӣЁоҶҢ #{chunk.chunk_index}</span>
                        </div>
                        <pre>{chunk.content}</pre>
                      </article>
                    ))}
                    {knowledgeBasePreviewChunks.length === 0 ? (
                      <div className="feedback-banner">жқ©ж¬Һе”ӨйҸӮеӣЁгҖӮйҸҶеӮӣжӨӮеЁҢв„ғж№ҒйҚҷоҲҡзқҚз»Җиҷ№ж®‘йҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗйҗ—еӣЁоҶҢйҠҶ?/div>
                    ) : null}
                  </div>
                )}
              </section>
            </div>
          ) : null}

          {panelEditModal ? (
            <div className="admin-edit-modal-backdrop" onClick={closePanelEditModal} role="presentation">
              <section
                aria-labelledby="panel-edit-modal-title"
                aria-modal="true"
                className="admin-edit-modal"
                onClick={(event) => {
                  event.stopPropagation();
                }}
                role="dialog"
              >
                <div className="admin-edit-modal-header">
                  <div>
                    <p className="section-eyebrow">еҜ®еңӯзҚҘзјӮж ¬з·«</p>
                    <h2 id="panel-edit-modal-title">
                      {panelEditModal === "plan" ? (planEditor.id > 0 ? "з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈжөјж°¬жҶійҸӮи§„о”Қ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғжөјж°¬жҶійҸӮи§„о”Қ") : null}
                      {panelEditModal === "subscription" ? "з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈжөјж°¬жҶійҸҲе¶…е§ҹйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬? : null}
                      {panelEditModal === "learner" ? "з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈзҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’§еӢ¬жһЎ" : null}
                      {panelEditModal === "admin" ? (adminEditor.id > 0 ? "з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈйҚҡеәЎеҪҙз’җп№ҖеҪҝ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғйҚҡеәЎеҪҙз’җп№ҖеҪҝ") : null}
                      {panelEditModal === "role" ? (roleEditor.id > 0 ? "з’ӢеҶ©жҡЈе®ҖжӨҫз¶…йҸүеҶ®жӘәеҰҜв„ғжҫҳ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғе®ҖжӨҫз¶…йҸүеҶ®жӘәеҰҜв„ғжҫҳ") : null}
                    </h2>
                  </div>
                  <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                    йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙ
                  </button>
                </div>

                {panelEditModal === "plan" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSavePlan}>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸӮи§„о”ҚзјӮж «зҲң</span>
                      <input
                        disabled={planEditor.id > 0}
                        value={planEditor.key}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, key: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="english-monthly"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҚ“е¶…еҪҙзҒһжӣ гҒҡйҚҡе¶ҮРһ</span>
                      <input
                        value={planEditor.name}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, name: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="й‘»иҫ«оҮўйҸҲе қе®іжөјж°¬жҶі"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>йҸҖжғ°еһӮйҸӮз‘°зҙЎ</span>
                        <select
                          value={planEditor.billingMode}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, billingMode: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        >
                          <option value="monthly">йҺёеӨӢж№Җжөјж°¬жҶі</option>
                          <option value="lifetime">ж¶“вӮ¬еЁҶв„ғвӮ¬СӮжӢұйҸӮ?/option>
                        </select>
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>йҚһоҶ»зҺҜй”ӣе қеҺ“й”ӣ?/span>
                        <input
                          inputMode="decimal"
                          value={planEditor.priceYuan}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, priceYuan: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                          placeholder="19.90"
                        />
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸӮи§„о”Қз’Үеӯҳж§‘</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={3}
                        value={planEditor.description}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, description: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸҖиҲөоғҷеЁ“зҠ»дәҫзјӮж «зҲң</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={3}
                        value={planEditor.paymentChannels}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, paymentChannels: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder={"wechat\nwechat_native"}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>зҖӣп№ҖжҶійҚҷоҲқе№ҸеҜ°жҘғж®‘йҸүеҶӘжіӯ</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={4}
                        value={planEditor.features}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, features: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder={"жҘӮж©Җо•¶з’Үе¶…о„ҹж¶”зҮ¶nйҚҰзғҳж«ҷйҚ’е—ҷиў«\nйҺёдҪәз”»йҸҮеӯҳжҹҠ"}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="checkbox-field">
                      <input
                        checked={planEditor.recommended}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setPlanEditor((current) => ({ ...current, recommended: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      <span>йҚ“е¶…еҪҙйҸҚеӣӘоҶҮж¶“зғҳеё№й‘Ҫж„ӯжҹҹеҰ—?/span>
                    </label>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "plan"} type="submit">
                        {busyAction === "plan" ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёж¶“?.." : planEditor.id > 0 ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“ЁйҸӮи§„о”Қ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғйҸӮи§„о”Қ"}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}

                {panelEditModal === "subscription" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveSubscription}>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>зҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ</span>
                        <input disabled value={subscriptionEditor.customerRef} />
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>йҺөвӮ¬зҒһзӮөоқ–йҗ©?/span>
                        <input disabled value={formatSubjectLabel(subscriptionEditor.subjectKey)} />
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>еҜ®вӮ¬й–«ж°ӯжҹҹеҰ—?/span>
                        <select
                          value={subscriptionEditor.planKey}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, planKey: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        >
                          {plans.map((plan) => (
                            <option key={plan.key} value={plan.key}>
                              {plan.name} ({plan.key})
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>йҸҲе¶…е§ҹйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/span>
                        <select
                          value={subscriptionEditor.status}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, status: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        >
                          <option value="active">йҗўзҶёжҷҘж¶“?/option>
                          <option value="pending">еҜ°е‘Ҝж•“йҸҒ?/option>
                          <option value="expired">е®ёиҢ¶з№ғйҸҲ?/option>
                          <option value="cancelled">е®ёжҸ’еҪҮеЁ‘?/option>
                        </select>
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <label className="checkbox-field">
                      <input
                        checked={subscriptionEditor.autoRenew}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, autoRenew: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      <span>йҸҚеӣӘоҶҮж¶“йёҝеҡңйҚ”г„§з”»з’җеңӯж•ӨйҺҙ?/span>
                    </label>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>еҜ®вӮ¬й–«ж°ӯжӨӮй—Ӯ?/span>
                        <input
                          type="datetime-local"
                          value={subscriptionEditor.startedAt}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, startedAt: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        />
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>иӨ°ж’іеў йҸҲе¶…е§ҹйҚӣг„Ұж№ЎеҜ®вӮ¬жҝ®?/span>
                        <input
                          type="datetime-local"
                          value={subscriptionEditor.currentPeriodStart}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, currentPeriodStart: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        />
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>иӨ°ж’іеў йҸҲе¶…е§ҹйҚӣг„Ұж№ЎзјҒж’ҙжҪ«</span>
                        <input
                          type="datetime-local"
                          value={subscriptionEditor.currentPeriodEnd}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, currentPeriodEnd: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        />
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>зјҒе ҹо„ӣйҸғе •жЈҝ</span>
                        <input
                          type="datetime-local"
                          value={subscriptionEditor.cancelledAt}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setSubscriptionEditor((current) => ({ ...current, cancelledAt: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        />
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "subscription-save"} type="submit">
                        {busyAction === "subscription-save" ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёж¶“?.." : "ж·ҮжҝҶз“ЁйҸҲе¶…е§ҹйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}

                {panelEditModal === "learner" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveLearnerUser}>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>зҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ</span>
                      <input disabled value={learnerEditor.username} />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸ„з”өРһ</span>
                      <input
                        disabled={!canManageLearners}
                        value={learnerEditor.displayName}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setLearnerEditor((current) => ({ ...current, displayName: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>з’җп№ҖеҪҝйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/span>
                      <select
                        disabled={!canManageLearners}
                        value={learnerEditor.status}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setLearnerEditor((current) => ({ ...current, status: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      >
                        <option value="active">йҚҡоҲңж•Ө</option>
                        <option value="disabled">йҚӢж»…ж•Ө</option>
                      </select>
                    </label>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "learner-user"} type="submit">
                        {busyAction === "learner-user" ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёж¶“?.." : "ж·ҮжҝҶз“ЁзҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’§еӢ¬жһЎ"}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}

                {panelEditModal === "admin" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveAdminUser}>

                        }}
                        placeholder="content-manager"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҺҙж„¬жҶіжҝ®ж’іжӮ•</span>
                      <input
                        value={adminEditor.displayName}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAdminEditor((current) => ({ ...current, displayName: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="йҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗжқ©ж„ҜжғҖ"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>{adminEditor.id > 0 ? "й–Іе¶Үз–ҶзҖөе—ҷзҲңй”ӣе қеҪІй–«еӨӣзҙҡ" : "йҗ§иҜІз¶ҚзҖөе—ҷзҲң"}</span>
                      <input
                        type="password"
                        value={adminEditor.password}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAdminEditor((current) => ({ ...current, password: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="й‘·еҶІзҡҜ 8 жөЈ?
                      />
                    </label>
                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>е®ҖжӨҫз¶…йҸүеҶ®жӘә</span>
                        <select
                          value={adminEditor.role}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            const nextRole = event.target.value;
                            setAdminEditor((current) => ({
                              ...current,
                              role: nextRole,
                              isSuper: nextRole === "super_admin" ? true : current.isSuper,
                            }));
                          }}
                        >
                          {roles.map((role) => (
                            <option key={role.key} value={role.key}>
                              {adminRoleLabel(role.key, role.name)}
                            </option>
                          ))}
                        </select>
                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>жөЈи·Ёж•ӨйҗҳиҲөвӮ¬?/span>
                        <select
                          value={adminEditor.status}
                          onChange={(event) => {
                            setAdminEditor((current) => ({ ...current, status: event.target.value }));
                          }}
                        >
                          <option value="active">йҚҡоҲңж•Ө</option>
                          <option value="disabled">йҚӢж»…ж•Ө</option>
                        </select>
                      </label>
                    </div>
                    <label className="checkbox-field">
                      <input
                        checked={adminEditor.isSuper}
                        disabled={adminEditor.role === "super_admin"}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAdminEditor((current) => ({ ...current, isSuper: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      <span>йҺәе ңз°ЈйҚҸг„§зҸҜйҸҲвӮ¬жҘӮжЁ»жҪҲй—„?/span>
                    </label>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "admin-user"} type="submit">
                        {adminEditor.id > 0 ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёз’җп№ҖеҪҝз’ӢеҶ©жҡЈ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғйҚҡеәЎеҪҙз’җп№ҖеҪҝ"}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}

                {panelEditModal === "role" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveRole}>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>е®ҖжӨҫз¶…зјӮж «зҲң</span>
                      <input
                        disabled={roleEditor.id > 0}
                        value={roleEditor.key}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setRoleEditor((current) => ({ ...current, key: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="ops-manager"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>е®ҖжӨҫз¶…йҚҡе¶ҮРһ</span>
                      <input
                        value={roleEditor.name}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setRoleEditor((current) => ({ ...current, name: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="жқ©ж„ҜжғҖзјҒеҝ•жӮҠ"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>й‘ұеІғзҹ—з’Үеӯҳж§‘</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={3}
                        value={roleEditor.description}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setRoleEditor((current) => ({ ...current, description: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸ„еү§гҒҡжӨӨе“„з°ӯ</span>
                      <input
                        value={roleEditor.sort}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setRoleEditor((current) => ({ ...current, sort: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="0"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <div className="form-field">
                      <span>е®ҖжӨҫз¶…й‘іи—үе§Ҹй‘јеҶЁжҙҝ</span>
                      <div className="permission-builder">
                        <div className="permission-builder-summary">
                          <strong>{roleHasFullPermission ? "е®ёеҸүе·ҝжөңе қеҸҸй–®г„ҘжӮ—йҚҷжӢҢе…ҳйҚ”? : `е®ёжҹҘвӮ¬еӨӢе«Ё ${rolePermissionSelections.length} жӨӨзЎ…е…ҳйҚ”жІ—}</strong>
                          <p>йҗ©еӯҳеёҙйҚ•й№ғвӮ¬еӨүз¬ҹйҚ”ВӨе…ҳйҚ”ж¶ҳеөҶйҚҷоҲӨзҙқз»ҜиҚӨзІәжөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„Өз№ҡзҖӣжЁ»жҪҲй—„ж„°еҺӨзјғоҮҶзҙқж¶“е¶үжё¶з‘•дҪ№еўңйҚ”г„ҘпҪһйҚҗж¬җеҰ§йҸҲоҲңзҙӘйҗ®дҪөвӮ¬?/p>
                        </div>

                        {rolePermissionSelections.length > 0 ? (
                          <div className="tag-list">
                            {rolePermissionSelections.map((permission) => (
                              <span className="tag" key={permission}>
                                {permissionLabel(permission)}
                              </span>
                            ))}
                          </div>
                        ) : (
                          <p className="helper-text">жҝЎеӮӣзҒүжқ©ж¬ҺйҮңе®ҖжӨҫз¶…йҸҶеӮӣжӨӮеЁҢв„ғж№Ғжө и®із¶ҚйҺҝе¶„з¶”й‘іи—үе§Ҹй”ӣеұҪеҪІжө гғҘеҺӣж¶“е¶…е¬Җй–«еӨҲвӮ¬?/p>
                        )}

                        {roleUnknownPermissions.length > 0 ? (
                          <div className="feedback-banner">
                            иӨ°ж’іеў е®ҖжӨҫз¶…жқ©жЁәеҜҳйҚҡоӮўзҡҜй–ІеҝӣзҸ®з»ҫС„жҪҲй—„ж„¶зҙқйҸҶеӮӣжӨӮеЁҢв„ғж№ҒйҚҷоҲқоқӢйҚ–ж ¬оҮ©йҸ„еәҜзҙқж·ҮжҝҶз“ЁйҸғжңөзҙ°й‘·оҒ„е§©ж·ҮжҝҲжҡҖй”ӣ?                            <div className="tag-list">
                              {roleUnknownPermissions.map((permission) => (
                                <span className="tag" key={permission}>
                                  {permissionLabel(permission)}
                                </span>
                              ))}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        ) : null}

                        <div className="permission-group-grid">
                          {rolePermissionGroups.map((group) => (
                            <section className="permission-group-card" key={group.title}>
                              <div className="permission-group-header">
                                <strong>{group.title}</strong>
                                <span>{group.helper}</span>
                              </div>
                              <div className="permission-option-list">
                                {group.options.map((option) => {
                                  const checked = selectedRolePermissionSet.has(option.code);
                                  const disabled = roleHasFullPermission && option.code !== "*";

                                  return (
                                    <label
                                      className={
                                        checked
                                          ? "permission-option permission-option-selected"
                                          : disabled
                                            ? "permission-option permission-option-disabled"
                                            : "permission-option"
                                      }
                                      key={option.code}
                                    >
                                      <input
                                        checked={checked}
                                        className="permission-option-input"
                                        disabled={disabled}
                                        onChange={(event) => {
                                          toggleRolePermission(option.code, event.target.checked);
                                        }}
                                        type="checkbox"
                                      />
                                      <div className="permission-option-body">
                                        <strong>{option.label}</strong>
                                        <span>{option.description}</span>
                                      </div>
                                    </label>
                                  );
                                })}
                              </div>
                            </section>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "admin-role"} type="submit">
                        {roleEditor.id > 0 ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёе®ҖжӨҫз¶…еҰҜв„ғжҫҳ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғе®ҖжӨҫз¶…еҰҜв„ғжҫҳ"}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closePanelEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}
              </section>
            </div>
          ) : null}

          {apiConfigModalOpen ? (
            <div className="admin-edit-modal-backdrop" onClick={closeAPIConfigModal} role="presentation">
              <section
                aria-labelledby="api-config-modal-title"
                aria-modal="true"
                className="admin-edit-modal api-config-modal"
                onClick={(event) => {
                  event.stopPropagation();
                }}
                role="dialog"
              >
                <div className="admin-edit-modal-header">
                  <div>
                    <p className="section-eyebrow">API е®ёгғҘеҸҝеҜ®еңӯзҚҘ</p>
                    <h2 id="api-config-modal-title">{apiConfigEditor.id > 0 ? "зјӮж ¬з·« API е®ёгғҘеҸҝ" : "йҸӮжқҝо–ғ API е®ёгғҘеҸҝ"}</h2>
                  </div>
                  <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={closeAPIConfigModal} type="button">
                    йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙ
                  </button>
                </div>

                <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveAPIConfig}>
                  <div className="form-grid-two">
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҚҡе¶ҮРһ</span>
                      <input
                        value={apiConfigEditor.name}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, name: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="жёҡе¬Әоӣ§й”ӣж°ӯзң№йҗңеӣЁз…Ўз’Ү?
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>MCP е®ёгғҘеҸҝйҚҡ?/span>
                      <input
                        value={apiConfigEditor.tool_name}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, tool_name: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="жёҡе¬Әоӣ§й”ӣжӯҹxchange_rate_query"
                      />
                    </label>
                  </div>

                  <div className="feedback-banner">жқ©ж¬“еҷ·йҺёеӨҠеј¬йҸҒдјҙвӮ¬ж„°гҖҚжҝүоӮўе•“йҚ—еҶІеҪІй”ӣеұјз¬…й—ҲгҲўж®‘ JSON жөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„§ж•“йҺҙж„¶зҙқж¶“е¶үжё¶з‘•дҪ№еўңйҚ”г„Ҙе•“йҠҶ?/div>

                  {getAPIConfigTestRows(apiConfigTestTarget).length > 0 ? (
                    <section className="api-test-parameter-builder">
                      <div className="api-test-parameter-list">
                        {getAPIConfigTestRows(apiConfigTestTarget).map((row) => (
                          <label className="form-field api-test-parameter-field" key={row.name}>
                            <span>
                              {row.name}
                              {row.required ? " *" : ""}
                            </span>
                            <small className="helper-text">
                              {row.description || (row.location === "url" ? "URL йҚҷеӮӣжҡҹ" : row.location === "body" ? "з’Үй”Ӣзң°жөЈж’іеј¬йҸҒ? : "з’Үй”Ӣзң°жҫ¶жқ‘еј¬йҸҒ?)}
                            </small>

                            {row.type === "object" ? (
                              <textarea
                                rows={6}
                                value={apiConfigTestValues[row.name] ?? ""}
                                onChange={(event) => {
                                  updateAPIConfigTestValue(row.name, event.target.value);
                                }}
                                placeholder='{"key":"value"}'
                              />
                            ) : row.type === "boolean" ? (
                              <select
                                value={apiConfigTestValues[row.name] ?? "true"}
                                onChange={(event) => {
                                  updateAPIConfigTestValue(row.name, event.target.value);
                                }}
                              >
                                <option value="true">true</option>
                                <option value="false">false</option>
                              </select>
                            ) : (
                              <input
                                type={row.type === "number" ? "number" : "text"}
                                value={apiConfigTestValues[row.name] ?? ""}
                                onChange={(event) => {
                                  updateAPIConfigTestValue(row.name, event.target.value);
                                }}
                                placeholder={row.exampleValue || `з’Үз–Ҝз·ӯйҚҸ?${row.name}`}
                              />
                            )}
                          </label>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </section>
                  ) : null}

                  <label className="form-field">
                    <span>з’Үй”Ӣзң°йҚҰжқҝжҪғ</span>
                    <input
                      value={apiConfigEditor.url}
                      onChange={(event) => {
                        setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, url: event.target.value }));
                      }}
                      placeholder="https://example.com/api"
                    />
                  </label>

                  <div className="form-grid-two">
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>з’Үй”Ӣзң°йҸӮи§„зЎ¶</span>
                      <select
                        value={apiConfigEditor.method}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, method: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      >
                        <option value="GET">GET</option>
                        <option value="POST">POST</option>
                        <option value="PUT">PUT</option>
                        <option value="PATCH">PATCH</option>
                        <option value="DELETE">DELETE</option>
                        <option value="HEAD">HEAD</option>
                      </select>
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҚ’е—ҷиў«</span>
                      <input
                        value={apiConfigEditor.category}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, category: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="жёҡе¬Әоӣ§й”ӣж°ӯзҘҙз’Ү?/ йҸҢгғЁоҮ— / ж¶“ж°¬е§ҹ"
                      />
                    </label>
                  </div>

                  <label className="form-field">
                    <span>з’Үеӯҳж§‘</span>
                    <textarea
                      rows={3}
                      value={apiConfigEditor.description}
                      onChange={(event) => {
                        setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, description: event.target.value }));
                      }}
                      placeholder="з» вӮ¬йҚ—жӣЎоҮ©йҸ„еәӨз№–ж¶“оҒ…еёҙйҚҷпҪҶж§ёйҚӢж°«зІҲж¶”е ўж®‘йҠҶдҫҖвӮ¬еӮҡжӮҺжө вӮ¬ж¶”е қжәҖйҸ…оҲқзҡҹйҗўг„ЈвӮ¬?
                    />
                  </label>

                  <div className="button-row">
                    <label className="tag">
                      <input
                        checked={apiConfigEditor.is_active}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, is_active: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      йҚҡоҲңж•Ө
                    </label>
                    <label className="tag">
                      <input
                        checked={Boolean(apiConfigEditor.is_public)}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, is_public: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      йҚҸо„Җзҙ‘
                    </label>
                    <label className="tag">
                      <input
                        checked={Boolean(apiConfigEditor.allow_admin_publish)}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigEditor((current) => ({ ...current, allow_admin_publish: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      йҚҸдҪҪоҶҸжө пҪ…еҪӮ
                    </label>
                  </div>

                  <section className="api-parameter-builder">
                    <div className="api-parameter-builder-header">
                      <div>
                        <h3>йҺәгғҘеҪӣйҚҷеӮӣжҡҹ</h3>
                        <p className="helper-text">йҺёеӨҠеј¬йҸҒжқҝжӮ•йҠҶдҪәиў«йҚЁе¬ЁвӮ¬дҪ·з¶…зјғоҶјжӢ°з’Үеӯҳж§‘еЁЈиҜІе§һй”ӣеІҖйғҙзјҒзҶ¶зҙ°й‘·оҒ„е§©йҗўзҶёеһҡ URL йҚҷеӮӣжҡҹйҠҶдҪҪоҮ¬е§№еӮҷз¶ӢйҚңеІғоҮ¬е§№еӮҡгҒ”йҠҶ?/p>
                      </div>
                      <button
                        className="secondary-button small-button"
                        onClick={() => {
                          addAPIConfigParameterRow();
                        }}
                        type="button"
                      >
                        еЁЈиҜІе§һйҚҷеӮӣжҡҹ
                      </button>
                    </div>

                    <div className="api-parameter-list">
                      {apiConfigParameterRows.map((row) => (
                        <div className="api-parameter-card" key={row.id}>
                          <div className="api-parameter-row">
                            <input
                              placeholder="йҚҷеӮӣжҡҹйҚҡ?
                              value={row.name}
                              onChange={(event) => {
                                updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, { name: event.target.value });
                              }}
                            />
                            <select
                              value={row.type}
                              onChange={(event) => {
                                updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, {
                                  type: normalizeAPIParameterType(event.target.value),
                                });
                              }}
                            >
                              {apiParameterTypeOptions.map((option) => (
                                <option key={option.value} value={option.value}>
                                  {option.label}
                                </option>
                              ))}
                            </select>
                            <select
                              value={row.location}
                              onChange={(event) => {
                                updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, {
                                  location: normalizeAPIParameterLocation(event.target.value),
                                });
                              }}
                            >
                              {apiParameterLocationOptions.map((option) => (
                                <option key={option.value} value={option.value}>
                                  {option.label}
                                </option>
                              ))}
                            </select>
                            <input
                              placeholder="йҚҷеӮӣжҡҹйҺ»еҝҡе Ә"
                              value={row.description}
                              onChange={(event) => {
                                updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, { description: event.target.value });
                              }}
                            />
                            <label className="checkbox-field api-parameter-required">
                              <input
                                checked={row.required}
                                onChange={(event) => {
                                  updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, { required: event.target.checked });
                                }}
                                type="checkbox"
                              />
                              <span>и№Үе‘ӯпҪһ</span>
                            </label>
                            <button
                              className="secondary-button small-button api-parameter-delete"
                              onClick={() => {
                                removeAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id);
                              }}
                              type="button"
                            >
                              йҚ’зҠ»ж«Һ
                            </button>
                          </div>
                          <div className="api-parameter-example">
                            <label className="form-field">
                              <span>еЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜз»ҖиҪ°з·ҘйҚҠ?/span>
                              <input
                                placeholder={row.type === "object" ? '{"keyword":"value"}' : "ж·ҮжҝҶз“ЁйҚҡеәЈеҒЈеЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜжөјж°іеҡңйҚ”г„Ҙз”«йҚ‘йёҝз№–ж¶“оҒ„вӮ¬?}
                                value={row.exampleValue}
                                onChange={(event) => {
                                  updateAPIConfigParameterRow(row.id, { exampleValue: event.target.value });
                                }}
                              />
                            </label>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </section>

                  <details
                    className="api-config-advanced"
                    onToggle={(event) => {
                      setAPIConfigAdvancedOpen((event.currentTarget as HTMLDetailsElement).open);
                    }}
                    open={apiConfigAdvancedOpen}
                  >
                    <summary>жҘӮжЁјйӘҮз’Ғеү§з–Ҷй”ӣе қеҪІй–«еӨӣзҙҡ</summary>
                    <p className="helper-text">йҚҷоҒ…ж№Ғй–¬еӣ§еҹҢйҚҘе“„з•ҫз’Үй”Ӣзң°жҫ¶ж·¬вӮ¬дҪёоҳІйҸүеӮқоҮ¬е§№еӮҷз¶ӢйҠҶдҪәо„·йҚҡе¶…з“§еЁҲдҪғз№–жөңж¶ҡеЈ’еЁҲе©ӮжәҖйҸ…оҲӣжӨӮй”ӣеұҫеў й—ҮвӮ¬з‘•дҪёзқҚеҜ®вӮ¬жҝүоӮўе•“йҠҶ?/p>

                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>жЈ°жҝҶоҳ»з’Үй”Ӣзң°жҫ¶?JSON</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={5}
                        value={apiConfigAdvancedHeaders}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigAdvancedHeaders(event.target.value);
                        }}
                        placeholder='{"Authorization":"Bearer {{token}}"}'
                      />
                    </label>

                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>жЈ°жҝҶоҳ»з’Үй”Ӣзң°жөЈ?JSON</span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={6}
                        value={apiConfigAdvancedBody}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setAPIConfigAdvancedBody(event.target.value);
                        }}
                        placeholder='{"fixed_key":"fixed_value"}'
                      />
                    </label>
                  </details>

                  <div className="button-row">
                    <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "admin-api-config-save"} type="submit">
                      {busyAction === "admin-api-config-save"
                        ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёж¶“?.."
                        : apiConfigEditor.id > 0
                          ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ё API е®ёгғҘеҸҝ"
                          : "еЁЈиҜІе§һ API е®ёгғҘеҸҝ"}
                    </button>
                    <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closeAPIConfigModal} type="button">
                      йҚҷж Ёз§·
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </form>
              </section>
            </div>
          ) : null}

          {apiConfigTestTarget ? (
            <div className="admin-edit-modal-backdrop" onClick={closeAPIConfigTestModal} role="presentation">
              <section
                aria-labelledby="api-config-test-modal-title"
                aria-modal="true"
                className="admin-edit-modal api-test-modal"
                onClick={(event) => {
                  event.stopPropagation();
                }}
                role="dialog"
              >
                <div className="admin-edit-modal-header">
                  <div>
                    <p className="section-eyebrow">еЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜйҸҒзүҲеөҒеҜ®еңӯзҚҘ</p>
                    <h2 id="api-config-test-modal-title">еЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜ API е®ёгғҘеҸҝ</h2>
                  </div>
                  <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={closeAPIConfigTestModal} type="button">
                    йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙ
                  </button>
                </div>

                <div className="api-test-meta">
                  <div>
                    <span>е·Ҙе…·еҗҚз§°</span>
                    <strong>{apiConfigTestTarget.name}</strong>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span>MCP е·Ҙе…·еҗҚ</span>
                    <strong>{apiConfigTestTarget.resolved_tool_name}</strong>
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span>иҜ·жұӮж–№ејҸ</span>
                    <strong>{apiConfigTestTarget.method}</strong>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <form
                  className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form"
                  onSubmit={(event) => {
                    event.preventDefault();
                    void handleTestAPIConfig(apiConfigTestTarget);
                  }}
                >
                  <div className="feedback-banner">
                    зңҹе®һеҸӮж•°еҖјиҰҒеЎ«еҶҷеңЁиҝҷйҮҢпјҢдёҚжҳҜдёҠйқўзҡ„вҖңеҸӮж•°жҸҸиҝ°вҖқгҖӮеҪ“еүҚжҺҘеҸЈиҮіе°‘йңҖиҰҒдј 
                    {` ${buildAPIParameterEditorState(apiConfigTestTarget)
                      .rows.filter((row) => row.name.trim())
                      .map((row) => row.name)
                      .join("гҖҒ") || "жөӢиҜ•еҸӮж•°"}`}
                    гҖӮ
                  </div>

                  <label className="form-field">
                    <span>йҗўзҶёеһҡйҗЁеӢ¬зҘҙз’Үжӣһеј¬йҸҒ?JSONй”ӣе ЈеҡңйҚ”г„§ж•“йҺҙж„¶зҙҡ</span>
                    <textarea
                      rows={12}
                      value={apiConfigTestArguments}
                      readOnly
                      placeholder='{"keyword":"з’Үз–Ҝз·ӯйҚҸгғ§ж№ЎзҖ№зӮәо•Ҫйҗ©?}'
                    />
                  </label>

                  {apiConfigTestResult ? (
                    <div className="api-test-response">
                      <div className="feedback-banner">
                        <strong>йҸҲвӮ¬жқ©жҲңз«ҙеЁҶпј„е§ёйҺ¬дҫҠзҙ°</strong> {apiConfigTestResult.status_code}
                      </div>
                      <pre className="code-panel">
                        {JSON.stringify(apiConfigTestResult.body ?? apiConfigTestResult.raw_body ?? apiConfigTestResult, null, 2)}
                      </pre>
                    </div>
                  ) : (
                    <div className="feedback-banner">жқҲж’іеҸҶеЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜйҚҷеӮӣжҡҹйҚҡеәЈеҒЈйҚ‘зғ©вӮ¬ж»ғзҙ‘жҝ®е¬«зҘҙз’Үжӣ—вӮ¬жҝ“зҙқжқ©ж–ҝжҙ–зјҒж’ҙзҒүжөјж°ӯжЁүз»Җе“„ж№Әжқ©ж¬ҺйҮңеҜ®еңӯзҚҘй–Іеұ»вӮ¬?/div>
                  )}

                  <div className="button-row">
                    <button
                      className="primary-button"
                      disabled={busyAction === `admin-api-config-test-${apiConfigTestTarget.id}`}
                      type="submit"
                    >
                      {busyAction === `admin-api-config-test-${apiConfigTestTarget.id}` ? "еЁҙе¬ӯзҳҜж¶“?.." : "еҜ®вӮ¬жҝ®е¬«зҘҙз’Ү?}
                    </button>
                    <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closeAPIConfigTestModal} type="button">
                      йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙеҜ®еңӯзҚҘ
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </form>
              </section>
            </div>
          ) : null}

          {contentEditModal ? (
            <div className="admin-edit-modal-backdrop" onClick={closeContentEditModal} role="presentation">
              <section
                aria-labelledby="content-edit-modal-title"
                aria-modal="true"
                className="admin-edit-modal"
                onClick={(event) => {
                  event.stopPropagation();
                }}
                role="dialog"
              >
                <div className="admin-edit-modal-header">
                  <div>
                    <p className="section-eyebrow">иӨ°ж’іеў жӨӨз”өзҙӘжқҲ?/p>
                    <h2 id="content-edit-modal-title">
                      {contentEditModal === "subject" ? "зјӮж ¬з·«зҖӣпёҝзҜ„з»үжҲ жҙ°" : null}
                      {contentEditModal === "category" ? "зјӮж ¬з·«йҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗйҚ’е—ҷзІҚ" : null}
                      {contentEditModal === "grade" ? "зјӮж ¬з·«зҖӣпёҝзҜ„й—ғиҲөоҶҢ" : null}
                      {contentEditModal === "word" ? "зјӮж ¬з·«йҚ—жӣЎзҳқйҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗ" : null}
                    </h2>
                  </div>
                  <button className="secondary-button small-button" onClick={closeContentEditModal} type="button">
                    йҚҸжҠҪжЈҙ
                  </button>
                </div>

                {contentEditModal === "subject" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveSubject}>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>з»үжҲ жҙ°зјӮж «зҲң</span>
                      <input
                        value={subjectForm.key}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubjectForm((current) => ({ ...current, key: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="english"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҚ“е¶…еҪҙйҸ„еү§гҒҡйҚҡе¶ҮРһ</span>
                      <input
                        value={subjectForm.name}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubjectForm((current) => ({ ...current, name: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="й‘»иҫ«оҮўжҘӮж©Җо•¶з’Үе¶Ҷзң№"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҸ„еү§гҒҡжӨӨе“„з°ӯ</span>
                      <input
                        inputMode="numeric"
                        value={subjectForm.sort}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubjectForm((current) => ({ ...current, sort: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                        placeholder="0"
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>з»үжҲ жҙ°з» вӮ¬жө ?/span>
                      <textarea
                        rows={3}
                        value={subjectForm.description}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubjectForm((current) => ({ ...current, description: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      />
                    </label>
                    <label className="checkbox-field">
                      <input
                        checked={subjectForm.featured}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setSubjectForm((current) => ({ ...current, featured: event.target.checked }));
                        }}
                        type="checkbox"
                      />
                      <span>йҚ“е¶…еҪҙжөјжЁәеҺӣзҒһжӣ гҒҡжқ©ж¬ҺйҮңз»үжҲ жҙ°</span>
                    </label>
                    <div className="button-row">
                      <button className="primary-button" disabled={busyAction === "subject"} type="submit">
                        {busyAction === "subject" ? "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёж¶“?.." : "ж·ҮжҝҶз“Ёз»үжҲ жҙ°"}
                      </button>
                      <button className="secondary-button" onClick={closeContentEditModal} type="button">
                        йҚҷж Ёз§·
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </form>
                ) : null}

                {contentEditModal === "category" ? (
                  <form className="setup-form admin-edit-modal-form" onSubmit={handleSaveCategory}>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>иӨ°жҺ‘зқҳз»үжҲ жҙ°</span>
                      <select
                        value={categoryForm.subjectKey}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setCategoryForm((current) => ({ ...current, subjectKey: event.target.value }));
                        }}
                      >
                        {subjects.map((subject) => (
                          <option key={subject.key} value={subject.key}>
                            {subject.name}
                          </option>
                        ))}
                      </select>
                    </label>
                    <label className="form-field">
                      <span>йҚ’е—ҷзІҚз»«иҜІзҖ·</span>
                      <input
                        value={categoryForm.kind}
                        onChange={(event) => {
                          setCategoryForm((current) => ({ ...current, kind: event.target.value }));

                        placeholder="topic"
                      />

                    <label className="form-field">

                      </label>
                      <label className="form-field">
                        <span>зҖӣпёҝзҜ„й—ғиҲөоҶҢ</span>
                        <select

                      />

                    <div className="form-grid-two">
                      <label className="form-field">

function SummaryCard(props: { label: string; value: string; help: string }) {
  return (
    <article className="summary-card">
      <p>{props.label}</p>
      <strong>{props.value}</strong>
      <span>{props.help}</span>
    </article>
  );
}

function DataTable(props: {
  columns: string[];
  rows: ReactNode[][];
  emptyText: string;
  wrapClassName?: string;
  tableClassName?: string;
}) {
  if (props.rows.length === 0) {
    return <div className="feedback-banner">{props.emptyText}</div>;
  }

  const wrapClassName = props.wrapClassName ? props.wrapClassName : "table-wrap";
  const tableClassName = props.tableClassName ? props.tableClassName : "data-table";

  return (
    <div className={wrapClassName}>
      <table className={tableClassName}>
        <thead>
          <tr>
            {props.columns.map((column) => (
              <th key={column}>{column}</th>
            ))}
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>
          {props.rows.map((row, index) => (
            <tr key={index}>
              {row.map((cell, cellIndex) => (
                <td key={`${index}-${cellIndex}`}>{cell}</td>
              ))}
            </tr>
          ))}
        </tbody>
      </table>
    </div>
  );
}

function AdminSectionTabs<K extends string>(props: {
  ariaLabel: string;
  currentKey: K;
  items: Array<WorkspaceTabItem<K>>;
  onChange: (key: K) => void;
}) {
  return (
    <div aria-label={props.ariaLabel} className="import-tabbar" role="tablist">
      {props.items.map((item) => (
        <button
          aria-selected={props.currentKey === item.key}
          className={props.currentKey === item.key ? "import-tab-button import-tab-button-active" : "import-tab-button"}
          key={item.key}
          onClick={() => props.onChange(item.key)}
          role="tab"
          title={item.helper ? `${item.label} и·Ҝ ${item.helper}` : item.label}
          type="button"
        >
          <span className="import-tab-label">{item.label}</span>
          {item.count !== undefined ? <em>{formatCount(item.count)}</em> : null}
        </button>
      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

function PagerControls(props: {
  page: number;
  total: number;
  pageSize: number;
  onChange: (page: number) => void;
  disabled?: boolean;
}) {
  const totalPages = Math.max(1, Math.ceil(props.total / Math.max(props.pageSize, 1)));

  return (
    <div className="pager">
      <button
        className="secondary-button small-button"
        disabled={props.disabled || props.page <= 1}
        onClick={() => props.onChange(Math.max(1, props.page - 1))}
        type="button"
      >
        ж¶“е©Ғз«ҙжӨӨ?      </button>
      <span>
        з»—?{props.page} / {totalPages} жӨӨ?      </span>
      <button
        className="secondary-button small-button"
        disabled={props.disabled || props.page >= totalPages}
        onClick={() => props.onChange(Math.min(totalPages, props.page + 1))}
        type="button"
      >
        ж¶“е¬©з«ҙжӨӨ?      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

function parsePermissionInput(value: string) {
  const seen = new Set<string>();
  const result: string[] = [];

  value
    .split(/[\n,]/)
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .forEach((item) => {
      if (seen.has(item)) {
        return;
      }
      seen.add(item);
      result.push(item);
    });

  return result;
}

function stringifyPermissionSelection(values: string[]) {
  const normalized = parsePermissionInput(values.join("\n"));
  const normalizedSet = new Set(normalized);
  const orderedKnownPermissions = rolePermissionCodeOrder.filter((permission) => normalizedSet.has(permission));
  const customPermissions = normalized.filter((permission) => !rolePermissionCodeSet.has(permission));
  return [...orderedKnownPermissions, ...customPermissions].join("\n");
}

function parseLineList(value: string) {
  const seen = new Set<string>();
  const result: string[] = [];

  value
    .split(/[\n,]/)
    .map((item) => item.trim())
    .filter(Boolean)
    .forEach((item) => {
      if (seen.has(item)) {
        return;
      }
      seen.add(item);
      result.push(item);
    });

  return result;
}

function toDateTimeLocalValue(value?: string) {
  if (!value) {
    return "";
  }
  const date = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
    return "";
  }
  const offset = date.getTimezoneOffset() * 60000;
  return new Date(date.getTime() - offset).toISOString().slice(0, 16);
}

function fromDateTimeLocalValue(value: string) {
  if (!value) {
    return "";
  }
  const date = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
    return "";
  }
  return date.toISOString();
}

function readStoredState<T>(key: string, fallback: T): T {
  try {
    const raw = window.localStorage.getItem(key);
    if (!raw) {
      return fallback;
    }
    return JSON.parse(raw) as T;
  } catch {
    return fallback;
  }
}

function yuanToCents(value: string) {
  const normalized = value.trim();
  if (!normalized) {
    return 0;
  }
  const amount = Number(normalized);
  if (!Number.isFinite(amount) || amount < 0) {
    return 0;
  }
  return Math.round(amount * 100);
}

function centsToYuanInput(value: number) {
  if (!Number.isFinite(value)) {
    return "0.00";
  }
  return (value / 100).toFixed(2);
}

function formatCount(value: number) {
  return new Intl.NumberFormat("zh-CN").format(value);
}

function formatPrice(value: number) {
  return `${(value / 100).toFixed(2)} йҚҸеғ ;
}

function formatDateTime(value: string) {
  const date = new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) {
    return "-";
  }
  return date.toLocaleString("zh-CN");
}

function formatFileSize(bytes?: number) {
  if (!bytes || bytes <= 0) {
    return "0 B";
  }
  if (bytes < 1024) {
    return `${bytes} B`;
  }
  if (bytes < 1024 * 1024) {
    return `${(bytes / 1024).toFixed(1)} KB`;
  }
  return `${(bytes / (1024 * 1024)).toFixed(2)} MB`;
}

function applyIconLink(href?: string) {
  const normalized = (href ?? "").trim();
  let link = document.querySelector('link[rel="icon"]') as HTMLLinkElement | null;
  if (!link) {
    link = document.createElement("link");
    link.setAttribute("rel", "icon");
    document.head.appendChild(link);
  }

  if (!normalized) {
    link.removeAttribute("href");
    return;
  }

  link.setAttribute("href", normalized);
}

function readFileAsDataUrl(file: File) {
  return new Promise<string>((resolve, reject) => {
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = () => {
      if (typeof reader.result === "string") {
        resolve(reader.result);
        return;
      }
      reject(new Error("invalid file result"));
    };
    reader.onerror = () => reject(reader.error ?? new Error("read file failed"));
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  });
}

function paymentStatusLabel(status?: string) {
  switch (status) {
    case "success":
      return "йҸҖоҲҷзІҜйҺҙж„¬е§ӣ";
    case "failed":
      return "йҸҖоҲҷзІҜжҫ¶иҫ«и§Ұ";
    case "closed":
      return "е®ёжҸ’еҸ§й—Ӯ?;
    default:
      return "еҜ°е‘®ж•®жө ?;
  }
}

function paymentStatusClass(status?: string) {
  switch (status) {
    case "success":
      return "pill-success";
    case "failed":
      return "pill-danger";
    case "closed":
      return "pill-muted";
    default:
      return "pill-warning";
  }
}

function subscriptionStatusClass(status?: string) {
  switch (status) {
    case "active":
      return "pill-success";
    case "cancelled":
      return "pill-danger";
    case "expired":
      return "pill-muted";
    case "pending":
      return "pill-warning";
    default:
      return "pill-danger";
  }
}

function subscriptionStatusLabel(status?: string) {
  switch (status) {
    case "active":
      return "йҗўзҶёжҷҘж¶“?;
    case "expired":
      return "е®ёиҢ¶з№ғйҸҲ?;
    case "pending":
      return "еҜ°е‘Ҝж•“йҸҒ?;
    case "cancelled":
      return "е®ёжҸ’еҪҮеЁ‘?;
    default:
      return status || "-";
  }
}

function looksLikeAuthError(message: string) {
  return /(authorization|token|expired|claims|unauthorized)/i.test(message);
}

function paymentChannelLabel(channel?: string) {
  switch (channel) {
    case "wechat_native":
      return "еҜ°оҶ»дҝҠйҺөоӮӨзҲңйҸҖоҲҷзІҜ";
    case "wechat_jsapi":
      return "еҜ°оҶ»дҝҠйҚҗе‘®ж•®жө ?;
    case "wechat_contract_pay":
      return "еҜ°оҶ»дҝҠй‘·оҒ„е§©зјҒо…ЎеһӮ";
    case "wechat":
      return "еҜ°оҶ»дҝҠйҸҖоҲҷзІҜ";
    case "bank":
      return "й–ҫжғ°о”‘йҚ—?;
    case "alipay":
      return "йҸҖоҲҷзІҜзҖ№?;
    case "cash":
      return "з»ҫеӨёз¬…йҸҖиҲөоғҷ";
    default:
      return channel || "-";
  }
}

function formatPaymentChannelLabels(channels: string[]) {
  if (!channels.length) {
    return "еҜ°оҶ»дҝҠйҸҖоҲҷзІҜ";
  }
  return channels.map((channel) => paymentChannelLabel(channel)).join(" / ");
}

function formatPaymentProviderLabel(provider?: string) {
  return paymentChannelLabel(provider);
}

    case "grade.write":
      return "з» пј„жӮҠзҖӣпёҝзҜ„й—ғиҲөоҶҢ";
    case "site.read":
      return "йҸҢгғ§ж№…з»”ж¬‘еҒЈзҒһжӣ гҒҡ";
    case "site.write":
      return "з» пј„жӮҠз»”ж¬‘еҒЈзҒһжӣ гҒҡ";

      return "йҸҢгғ§ж№…йҸҖоҲҷзІҜз’ҒгҲ еҙҹ";

    case "plan.write":
      return "з» пј„жӮҠйҸҖжғ°еһӮйҸӮи§„о”Қ";
    case "learner.read":

    case "learner.write":
      return "з» пј„жӮҠзҖӣп№ҖжҶіз’җп№ҖеҪҝ";
    case "mcp.read":

    case "mcp.write":
      return "з» пј„жӮҠ MCP йҺәгғҘеҸҶ";

function adminRoleLabel(roleKey: string, fallbackName?: string) {
  switch (roleKey) {
    case "super_admin":
      return "з»”ж¬‘еҒЈйҺ¬жҳҸзӨӢз’җпҪ„жұү";
    case "content_admin":
      return "йҚҗе‘ӯоҶҗжқ©ж„ҜжғҖ";
    case "viewer":
      return "йҸҒзүҲеөҒйҸҢгғ§ж№…";
    default:
      return fallbackName || roleKey;
  }
}

function noticeDialogToneClass(tone: NoticeDialogTone) {
  switch (tone) {
    case "success":
      return "pill-success";
    case "warning":
      return "pill-warning";
    case "error":
      return "pill-danger";
    default:
      return "pill-muted";
  }
}

function noticeDialogTitleTag(tone: NoticeDialogTone) {
  switch (tone) {
    case "success":
      return "йҺҝе¶„з¶”зҖ№еұҫеһҡ";
    case "warning":
      return "з’ҮйЈҺвҖҳз’Ғ?;
    case "error":
      return "й—ҮвӮ¬з‘•дҪёоҳ©йҗһ?;
    default:
      return "еЁ“в•…ОҳйҺ»ж„®гҒҡ";
  }
}
